* **Spoiler: Braizen Giant Robot (PL 12, 180 PP)**  
* Hide  
  **Abilities**

  **STR:** (12). **STA:** \-. **AGI:** 0\. **DEX:** 0\. **FGT:** 12\. **INT:** \-. **AWE:** 0\. **PRE:** \-.

  **Stats**

  **Attack:** \+12. **Damage:** \+12. **Dodge (2):** \+8. **Parry (2):** \+8. **Toughness:** \+16. **Fortitude:** IMMUNE. **Will:** \+12. **Init:** \+0.

  **Skills**

  Perception 10 (+10), Stealth 0 (-12).

  **Advantages**

  All Out Attack, Interpose, Power Attack.

  **Powers**

  **Giant:** Growth 12 {24}.

  **Robot:** Immunity 30 (Fortitude; Quirk 5 \[Is subject to Affects Object powers, but resists them with Toughness\]), Feature 1 (Possesses a Will defense, beginning at \-5, despite Absent Intellect), Enhanced Will 17 (Limited \[Non-Mind-Affecting powers\]) {35}.

  **Metal Body:** Protection 4 {4}.

  **Way Too Big:** Immunity 20 (Uncommon Resistances \[Defense, Strength, etc\]; Limited \[Half Effect\]) {10}.

  **Thrusters:** Flight 12 {24}.

  **Nanite Repair:** Regeneration 1 {1}.

  **Lead Shielding:** Impervious Toughness 16, Immunity 20 (All Technopathy Effects) {36+1}.

  **Alt \- Radioactive:** Affliction 9 (Impaired/Disabled; Fortitude; Reaction \[Start of Turn\], Burst Area, Limited Degree).

  **Weapons Systems:** 48-point Strength-discounted Array {48-12+5}.

  **Servo Strength:** Damage 12 Linked Affliction 12 (Dazed+Vulnerable/Stunned+Prone; Prowess; Burst Area 2, Extra Condition, Limited Degree).

  **Thruster Stomp:** Damage 12 (Secondary Effect) Linked Weaken Toughness 12 (Toughness) Linked Move Object 12 (Reduced Range \[Close\]).

  **Automated Gunports:** Damage 12 (Targeted Burst Area, Selective, Multiattack).

  **Radiation Wave:** Weaken All Abilities 12 (Fortitude; Broad, Simultaneous, Cone Area).

  **Radiation Beams:** Damage 12 (Ranged) Linked Affliction 12 (Impaired/Disabled/Transformed; Fortitude; Ranged).

  **Radiation Bomb:** Affliction 12 (Impaired/Disabled/Transformed; Fortitude; Ranged, Burst Area, Cumulative).

  **Calculations**

  Abilities \-6 \+ Defenses 2 \+ Skills 5 \+ Advantages 3 \+ Powers 176 \= **180 PP**

  **Notes**

  The warlords who control the greatest Pits in the Braizen Isles defend their holdings fiercely. A popular option for that is with giant military robots. Anyone who is surprised by this has *not been paying attention to the rest of this document*. While design conceits and weapons systems can vary, this is a fairly standard model. The entire robot is constructed out of Pit-irradiated metals and alloys, its entire body effectively its power source. Though it doesn't have all the sleek sensors and specialized weapons systems of more traditional military machines, it is bristling with a lot of guns and can unload the radioactive energies powering it into focused damaging beams or debilitating bursts.

  These robots are entirely encased in lead shielding to keep them from, you know, poisoning and mutating anyone who walks by, and stuff. Conveniently, this lead also entirely blocks any technopathic access. The lead shielding can nanotechnically disabled, causing the robot to again give off dangerous radiation. In the short term, exposure to the radiation will usually just sicken and debilitate, but it can potentially cause lasting health consequences or mutations. Unshielded robots are often used to guard important locations that don't require constant active personnel, like storage facilities. The robots can shield up when authorized entrants come by, but otherwise, the dangerous radiation serves as about an effective a keep out sign as the giant military robot itself.

* **Spoiler: Braizen Mutant Powerhouse (PL 12, 180 PP)**  
* Hide  
  **Abilities**

  **STR:** 16\. **STA:** 16\. **AGI:** 0\. **DEX:** 0\. **FGT:** 8\. **INT:** 0\. **AWE:** 0\. **PRE:** 0\.

  **Stats**

  **Attack:** \+8. **Damage:** \+16. **Dodge:** \+8. **Parry:** \+8. **Toughness:** \+16. **Fortitude:** \+16. **Will (8):** \+8. **Init:** \+0.

  **Skills**

  Intimidation 20 (+20), Perception 8 (+8).

  **Advantages**

  Accurate Attack, All Out Attack, Fast Grab, Improved Grab, Improved Hold, Interpose, Power Attack, Precise Attack (Close/Cover), Startle, Takedown 2\.

  **Powers**

  **Resilience:** Immunity 2 (Critical Hits), Regeneration 1 {3}.

  **Tentacles:** Extra Limbs 5, Elongation 4 (120'; Quirk \[Extra Limbs Only\]) {8+1}.

  **Alt \- Tentacle Scramble:** Speed 8\.

  **Horror:** Feature 1 (Penalty to Startle as a move action reduced to \-2) {1}.

  **Durability:** 15-point Array {15+4}.

  **Impervious:** Impervious Toughness 15\.

  **Stubborn:** Immunity 30 (Will; Limited \[Half Effect\]).

  **Immovable Object:** Immunity 15 (Defense-resisted Effects).

  **Rapid Recovery:** Enhanced Regeneration 9, Healing 2 (Restorative, Reduced Action 2 \[Free\], Limited \[Self Only\], Limited \[Restorative function only\]).

  **Shrug Off:** Immunity 60 (Fortitude, Will; Limited \[Half Effect\], Limited \[Afflictions Only\], Limited \[Recovery Checks Only\]).

  **Super-Strength:** 32-point Strength-discounted Array {32-16+5}.

  **Slam:** Damage 16 Linked Affliction 16 (Dazed+Impaired/Stunned+Disabled; Fortitude; Extra Condition, Limited Degree).

  **Smash:** Damage 16 Linked Weaken Toughness 16 (Alternate Resistance \[Toughness\]).

  **Awesome Blow:** Damage 16 Linked Move Object 16 (Contagious, Limited \[Only to knock targets back or down\], Reduced Range \[Close\]).

  **Horrific Strike:** Damage 16 (Improved Critical 2\) Linked Affliction 12 (Impaired/Disabled/Controlled; Will; Perception Area \[Sight\], Limited \[Impaired/Disabled only apply while in sight, Controlled can only force targets to flee or cower\]), Feature 2 (Fearless Advantage only gives a \+2 on saves vs. the Affliction; a properly-costed Immunity to Emotional Effects is required for full immunity).

  **Shockwave Clap:** Damage 12 (Cone Area, 8 ranks Secondary Effect).

  **Ground Pound:** Damage 12 (Burst Area, Limited \[Targets must be on same surface\]) Linked Affliction 12 (Dazed+Vulnerable/Stunned+Defenseless; Alternate Resistance \[Prowess\], Burst Area, Extra Condition, Limited Degree, Limited \[Targets must be on same surface\]) Linked Move Object 12 (Burst Area, Increased Mass 2, Limited \[Targets must be on same surface\], Limited \[Only to knock targets back or down\], Reduced Range \[Close\]).

  **Random Mutation:** Randomly roll one of the following (1d20). Such effects often modify Strength Damage \- if they do, also apply to the first four powers of the Super-Strength array, and make Shockwave Clap Cone Area 2 and full Secondary Effect, Ground Pound add Cumulative to the Affliction and \+4 Increased Mass to the Move Object, to account for array growth {16}.

  **(1) Beast Legs:** Speed 8, Leaping 8\.

  **(2) Wings:** Flight 16 (Wings).

  **(3) Worm:** Burrowing 13, Movement 1 (Slithering), Enhanced Advantages (Prone Fighting).

  **(4) Skittering:** Speed 8, Movement 4 (Wall Crawling 2, Trackless, Sure Footed).

  **(5) Acid:** Strength Damage gains Secondary Effect.

  **(6) Claws:** Strength Damage gains Linked Affliction 16 (Impaired/Disabled/Incapacitated; Fortitude). Slam instead gains Cumulative on the Affliction.

  **(7) Bite:** Strength Damage gains Concentration.

  **(8) Webs:** Strength Damage gains Linked Affliction 16 (Dazed/Stunned/Incapacitated; Alternate Resistance \[Prowess\], Cumulative, Limited \[Physical actions only\]).

  **(9) Poison:** Strength Damage gains Linked Weaken Stamina 16 (Fortitude).

  **(10) Rage:** Strength Damage gains Linked Weaken Chosen Defense 16 (Will; Broad, Limited \[Penalty only applies against self\]).

  **(11) Terrain-Warping Blows:** Strength Damage gains Linked Create 16 (Reduced Range \[Close\]); this applies fully to all arrayed effects, including the Area ones.

  **(12) Scales:** Impervious is moved out of the Durability Array, gains one rank. Enhanced Advantages (Defensive Attack).

  **(13) Madness:** Stubborn is moved out of the Durability Array. Enhanced Advantages 2 (Diehard, Fearless).

  **(14) Random Phasing:** Immovable Object is moved out of the Durability Array. Movement 1 (Permeate).

  **(15) Metabolism:** Rapid Recovery is moved outside of Durability Array; Speed 2\.

  **(16) Ferocity:** Shrug Off is moved out of the Durability Array. Enhanced Advantages 2 (Diehard, Fearless).

  **(17) Eyes Everywhere:** Senses 11 (Extended Rapid Analytical Vision, Vision Counters All Concealment, Vision Counters Illusion), Enhanced Perception 10\.

  **(18) Ears Everywhere:** Senses 9 (Extended Rapid Accurate Hearing, Hearing Counters All Concealment), Senses 4 (Hearing Penetrates Concealment; Limited \[Only for going around objects, not straight through them\]), Enhanced Perception 10\.

  **(19) Olfactory Maws:** Senses 11 (Ranged Acute Accurate Analytical Extended Smell, Smell Counters All Concealment), Enhanced Perception 10\.

  **(20) Stealth:** Concealment 4 (All Visual Senses; Passive); Teleport 4 (Limited \[Only while not in sight\]), Enhanced Stealth 16.\[/INDENT\]

  **Calculations**

  Abilities 80 \+ Defenses 8 \+ Skills 14 \+ Advantages 11 \+ Powers 51 \= **164 PP**

  **Notes**

  Braizen Pit Radiation can interact weirdly with Dreamer powers. It can cause Dreamer powers to weaken, change, vanish, or even (rarely) grow. Some fifteen years ago, an Ilessian scientist felt that a thorough study of this phenomenon was required. And oh, yes, she was a Dreamcatcher.

  Claiming a mid-sized Pit, establishing a secure base, and secretly kidnapping Ilessian Dreamers and transporting them to the Isles, she conducted her experiments. Initial results were unpromising, with most Dreamers seeing an overall reduction in total power, if not from the effects of the radiation itself, then from the loss of Spiritual Energy caused by prolonged exposure. Many of the subjects died, often due to complications when they lost Required Secondary Powers that kept their abilities from harming them or having other unforeseen effects. Some went mad and injured or killed themselves or others in blind fury. This was all marked down as "interesting data".

  However, the Dreamcatcher found that using cybernetic implants constructed of irradiated materials, along with certain drugs and treatments, could allow Dreamers to draw on the Braizen radiation itself to power their abilities, along with their Spiritual Energy. In fact, with the proper procedures, the odds of seeing an overall improvement in Dreamer abilities went up significantly. Granted, it meant the Dreamers subject to such treatments would suffer horrifying physical and mental transformations and become dependent on recharging on dangerous Braizen radiation for their own survival. But, you know, SCIENCE\! And stuff.

  Of course, in recent years, warped, twisted, and surprisingly powerful Dreamers have begun walking the Isles, seeking out Pits to recharge the dangerous cybernetics keeping them alive, often coming into conflict with natives or various other interests. Of the Dreamcatcher who performed the experiments, well, no one's really heard from her in years. No doubt these facts are entirely unrelated.

* **Spoiler: Hovertank (PL 12 Vehicle, 180 EP)**  
* Hide  
  **Basics**

  **Size:** H. **Strength:** 12\. **Defense:** \+8. **Toughness:** \+16. **Speed:** Flight 3 (Alt: Speed 6).

  **Features**

  Communications, Computer, Navigation System.

  **Powers**

  **Tactical Computers:** Enhanced Ranged Attack 4 (Affects Others Only) {4}.

  **Heavy Armor:** Impervious Toughness 16 {16}.

  **Power Dampeners:** Feature 2 (Possesses a Will and Fortitude Defense despite Absent Abilities, starting at \-5); Enhanced Will 17 (Limited \[Non-mental Effects\]), Enhanced Fortitude 17 (Limited \[Affects Objects powers\]) {19}.

  **Computer Security:** Immunity 10 (Technopathic Compulsions; Limited \[Half Effect\]) {5}.

  **Nanite Repair System:** Regeneration 11 {11}.

  **HUD:** Senses 6 (Radius Extended Vision Penetrates Concealment; Limited \[Mapping\]) {3}.

  **Sensor Suite:** Senses 5 (Vision Counters All Concealment) {5}.

  **Active Defense System:** Nullify Physical Projectiles 12 (Reaction \[When targeted by an appropriate effect\], Reduced Range \[Close\], Limited \[Counters Only\]) {24}.

  **Tank:** Immunity 7 (Slam Damage, Critical Hits) {7}.

  **Weapons Systems:** Create an array of four of the following plus Main Tank Cannon and Crush {48+5}.

  **Main Tank Cannon:** Damage 16 (Ranged, 12 ranks Burst Area, Improved Critical 4).

  **Crush:** Damage 12 (Burst Area, Limited \[Must first spend a move action getting into position above the target\]) Linked Move Object 12 (Burst Area, Limited, Reduced Range \[Close\]) Linked Weaken Toughness 12 (Toughness; Burst Area, Limited); Enhanced Trait 12 (Progressive on Weaken; Limited \[Only while a Grab is maintained\]).

  **Autolock Gattling Gun:** Damage 12 (Ranged, Multiattack, Concentration).

  **Incendiary Gattling Gun:** Damage 12 (Ranged, Multiattack, Secondary Effect).

  **Homing Gattling Gun:** Damage 12 (Multiattack, Targeted Cone Area, Accurate 6, Homing 2, Improved Critical 4).

  **Kinetic Cannon:** Damage 12 (Ranged) Linked Affliction 12 (Dazed+Impaired/Stunned+Disabled; Fortitude; Ranged, Extra Condition, Limited Degree).

  **Plasma Cannon:** Damage 12 (Ranged) Linked Weaken Toughness 12 (Toughness; Ranged).

  **Laser Cannon:** Damage 12 (Perception Range, Alternate Resistance \[Highest Base Active Defense\]).

  **Flame Blaster:** Damage 12 (Cone Area 2, Secondary Effect).

  **Electricity Blaster:** Damage 12 (Shapeable Area 2 \[Limited to 6"x6"x240' Line\]) Linked Affliction 12 (Vulnerable/Stunned/Incapacitated; Fortitude; Shapeable Area 2 \[Limited to 6"x6"x240' Line\]).

  **Sound Blaster:** Damage 12 (Burst Area) Linked Affliction 12 (Dazed/Stunned/Incapacitated; Will; Burst Area).

  **Guided Rocket Launcher:** Damage 14 (Ranged, 12 ranks Burst Area, Extended Range 6, Homing 2).

  **Grenade Launcher:** Damage 12 (Ranged, Burst Area) Linked Move Object 12 (Burst Area, Limited 2 \[Knockback Only\]).

  **Missile Launcher:** Damage 12 (Ranged, Burst Area 3, Unreliable \[5 Uses\]).

  **Calculations**

  Size 2 \+ Strength 4 \+ Defense 10 \+ Toughness 7 \+ Speed 7 \+ Features 3 \+ Powers 147 \= **180 EP**

  **Notes**

  Honestly, one of the biggest strengths of hovertanks is the sheer intimidation factor of having a huge, armored, absolutely-not-aerodynamic tank come flying your way. Or a squadron of them, as the case may be. Hovertanks can be equipped with pretty much all of the same weaponry (although they typically use heavier ordinance) as an ACV, as well as packing a heavy artillery cannon for really tough targets. Of course, in many cases, simply floating up above the enemy and dropping on it is plenty sufficient for dealing with a wide range of threats.

  Hovertanks are intended as heavy cavalry vehicles to break an assaulting military force. They don't have as many utility features as ACVs, but have extremely robust defensive systems, including high-end nanite repair functions and automated defense systems.

  Size 2 \+ Strength 2 \+ Defense 14 \+ Toughness 3 \+ Speed 26 \+ Features 4 \+ Powers 129 \= **180 EP**

  **Notes**

  Fighter jets are armed with more and stronger weapons than attack helicopters, and are significantly faster and more durable. They are also equipped with a neural link to camera systems that allow the pilot to take in visual data extremely rapidly, and accurately judge distances with a glance, valuable for complicated high-speed actions. Most importantly, fighter jets are space-capable, bringing an entirely new dimension to the battlefield.

* **Spoiler: Small-scale Mech (PL 12, 180 PP)**  
* Hide  
  **Abilities**

  **STR:** (12). **STA:** \-. **AGI:** 0\. **DEX:** 0\. **FGT:** 12\. **INT:** \-. **AWE:** 0\. **PRE:** \-.

  **Stats**

  **Attack:** \+12. **Damage:** \+12. **Dodge (6):** \+12. **Parry (6):** \+12. **Toughness:** \+12. **Fortitude:** IMMUNE. **Will:** \+12. **Init:** \+0.

  **Skills**

  Perception 18 (+18).

  **Advantages**

  By Pilot.

  **Powers**

  **Humongous Mecha:** Growth 12 (Permanent) {24}.

  **Power Dampeners:** Feature 1 (Possesses a Will defense despite absent Intellect, starting at \-5), Enhanced Will 17 (Limited \[Non-Mind-Affecting Effects\]) {10}.

  **Robot:** Immunity 30 (Fortitude) {30}.

  **Advanced Cyber Security:** Immunity 10 (Technopathic Compulsions; Quirk \[The technopath may choose to ignore this Immunity, but if it does, must roll a DC 35/30 Will save vs. Damage Linked Impaired/Disabled/Incapacitated Affliction Linked Weaken Will for each power attempt\]) {9}.

  **Piloted:** Feature 3 (The pilot gains a Dynamic Alternate Effect of its full list of Advantages, getting the same Advantages with Affects Others Only for the mech), Feature (The pilot's actions can originate from the mech in any round that the mech doesn't target anyone other than itself or the pilot with an action) {4}.

  **Imposing:** Enhanced Intimidation 8 (Affects Others) {4}.

  **Defense Systems:** 12-point Array {12+2}.

  **Nanite Repair:** Regeneration 11 {11}, Immunity 2 (Critical Hits; Limited \[Half Effect\]).

  **Forcefield:** Impervious Toughness 12\.

  **Cloaking System:** Concealment 6 (All Visual, All Auditory; Affects Self and Others).

  **Sensor Systems:** 8-point Array {8+2}.

  **Broad Spectrum Scanners:** Senses 6 (Extended Vision Counters All Concealment), Senses 4 (Vision Penetrates Concealment; Reduced Duration \[Concentration\]).

  **Tactical HUD:** Senses 8 (Extended 3 Radius Vision Penetrates Concealment; Limited \[Mapping\]), Senses 4 (Direction Sense, Distance Sense, Darkvision).

  **Target Scanner:** Senses 4 (Ranged Acute Analytical Detect \[Dreamer Powers\]), Senses 4 (Ranged Acute Analytical Detect \[Technology\]).

  **Mobility Systems:** 20-point Array {20+4}.

  **Jet Pack/Wing System:** Flight 15 (10 ranks Wings).

  **Space Travel:** Immunity 10 (Life Support; Affects Others), Flight 8 (Wings), Movement 1 (Space Travel).

  **Servo Motors:** Speed 10, Leaping 10\.

  **Smash Through:** Burrowing 16 (Limited \[Only for objects with Toughness less than or equal to rank\], Penetrating 12).

  **All Terrain:** Speed 10, Swimming 10\.

  **Weapons Systems:** 48-point Strength-discounted Array, choose five of the following plus Pilot Enhancement System {48-12+6}.

  **Pilot Enhancement System:** Variable 6 (Improve Existing Traits; Affects Others, Limited \[Pilot Only\]); not Strength Discounted.

  **Servo Strength:** Damage 12 (Multiattack) Linked Move Object 12 (Multiattack, Reduced Range \[Close\]).

  **Autolock Gattling Gun:** Damage 12 (Ranged, Multiattack, Concentration).

  **Suppressive Fire Expertise:** Damage 12 (Ranged, Multiattack) Linked Deflect 12\.

  **Autorockets:** Damage 12 (Ranged, Multiattack, Secondary Effect).

  **Kinetic Cannon:** Damage 12 (Ranged) Linked Affliction 12 (Dazed+Impaired/Stunned+Disabled; Fortitude; Ranged, Extra Condition, Limited Degree).

  **Plasma Cannon:** Damage 12 (Ranged) Linked Weaken Toughness 12 (Alternate Resistance \[Toughness\], Ranged).

  **Laser Cannon:** Damage 12 (Perception Range, Alternate Resistance \[Highest Base Active Defense\]).

  **Power Nullifiers:** Nullify Dreamer Powers 12 (Broad, Simultaneous).

  **Power Suppressors:** Affliction 12 (Entranced/Stunned/Transformed; Will; Ranged, Cumulative, Progressive, Limited \[Dreamer Powers Only\]).

  **Negation Grenades:** Affliction 12 (Entranced/Stunned/Transformed; Will; Ranged, Cloud Area, Secondary Effect, Cumulative, Limited \[Dreamer Powers Only\]).

  **Napalm Grenades:** Damage 12 (Ranged, Cloud Area, Secondary Effect).

  **Stun Grenades:** Affliction 12 (Dazed/Stunned/Incapacitated; Fortitude; Ranged, Burst Area, Cumulative).

  **Nanite Grenades:** Weaken Toughness 12 (Ranged, Burst Area, Alternate Resistance \[Highest Base Active Defense\]).

  **MechBlade:** Damage 12 Linked Affliction 12 (Impaired/Disabled/Incapacitated; Fortitude; Cumulative) Linked Weaken Toughness 12 (Toughness).

  **Laser Sword:** Damage 12 (Alternate Resistance \[Highest Active Defense\], Multiattack) Linked Deflect 12 (Multiattack, Reduced Range \[Close\]).

  **Energy Maul:** Damage 12 Linked Affliction 12 (Dazed/Stunned/Incapacitated; Fortitude; Cumulative) Linked Move Object 12 (Contagious, Reduced Range \[Close\], Limited \[Only to knock targets back or down\]).

  **Gunports:** Damage 12 (Targeted Burst Area, Multiattack, Selective)

  **Napalm Flame Thrower:** Damage 12 (Cone Area 2, Secondary Effect).

  **Pulse Generator:** Damage 12 (Burst Area) Linked Affliction 12 (Dazed+Vulnerable/Stunned+Defenseless; Fortitude; Burst Area, Extra Condition, Limited Degree).

  **Grenade Launcher:** Damage 12 (Ranged, Burst Area 2).

  **Rocket Launcher:** Damage 16 (Ranged, 12 ranks Burst Area, Extended Range 4, Homing 2, Inaccurate 2).

  **Missile Launcher:** Damage 12 (Ranged, Burst Area 3 \[Limited to other targets, only triggering if main target is hit\]).

  **Calculations**

  Abilities \-6 \+ Defenses 6 \+ Skills 9 \+ Advantages 0 \+ Powers 171 \= **180 PP**

  **Notes**

  Alright, let's discuss mechs.

  Mechs are one of the three main classes of "common" Aranthian superweapons, with the other two being nukes and kill sats. In terms of tactical function, mechs are more for taking and holding territory. They are what you use when you want a very precise application of a lot of power to clear out an entrenched enemy, and then secure that territory for yourself. So what makes mechs so powerful?

  First, mechs are extremely versatile. Whether flying through the air (at greater speeds than a fighter jet), standing guard over a secure location on the ground, plunging into the sea, or taking to the void of space, a mech will go wherever you need it to. Now, most of the weapons systems listed for the mech *can* be added to other military vehicles, but most of those Close range moves (which, less face it, are point-for-point more effective than ranged attacks due to the high speeds available in M\&M) are exclusive to them. Mechs are also more durable, taking damage as characters rather than objects. But the real advantage of the mech is its synergy with its pilot. Mechs are giant *humanoid* robots for a reason \- the way their energy is channeled mimics the natural flows of Spiritual Energy through a person's body. Combined with neural linking technology, piloting a mech is not just extremely intuitive, but all of the pilot's skills and capabilities can transfer to and be augmented by the mech \- *including Dreamer powers*.

  Mechanically, this is represented by that Pilot Enhancement System and the Piloted Features. The pilot can act through the mech, and the mech can augment the pilot. Most dedicated mech pilots (meaning, most mech pilots) will also have a power such as Ace Pilot, a similar Variable that works on its mech, allowing both to support each other or to just both be taking actions individually.

  Bear also in mind that the above template is the *smallest* and *weakest* version of the mech. A full scale mech is PL 15\. Larger mechs usually lack the Cloaking System, but have equivalent mobility, more resilience and attack power, and are often artificially intelligent, allowing them to operate independent of their pilot.

  **Playing a Mech:** First, a disclaimer. Additional characters are one of the most powerful things you can get in M\&M. Additional characters who are designed to augment a primary character are likely to do unpleasant things to PP balance. This is not a mechanical construct that is really recommended for most games.

  But you know what? Mech are awesome. So if you have a GM crazy enough to allow it, here's what you do

  So, you're in a PL 12 game and you want to play a mech pilot. But the mech isn't like a suit of powered armor, a single Removable device that leaves enough PP open to build a character with. What do you do?

  First, you have your pilot. The campaign is PL 12/180 PP, but you build your pilot as a completely standard PL 10/150 PP character. You can even grab one of the many PL 10 templates from above. Hero-level Paragon Mech Pilot. Dymaran Samurai Mech Pilot. Limbran Technomancer Mech Pilot. Whatever. (Probably not one of the powered armor guys though. That's just silly. OR IS IT\!?)

  To your pilot you then add...

  (Give it a second for the sane people to leave the room.)

  Enhanced Sidekick 36 (Removable).

  That's your mech. Note the default mechs have no Artificial Intelligence, so it's reasonable to be Removable \- it can't act without a pilot, so if the pilot is separated from its mech, the mech can't go on to complete a mission or seek the pilot out or whatever. Artifically intelligent mechs won't have Removable.

  Removable drops the cost there to only 29\. That leaves you one PP. Toss the aforementioned Ace Pilot Variable into your main combat array and you're good to go.

* **Spoiler: Dark Secrets of Mechanics Twisting. Open if you dare\!**

  **Notes**

  A full-scale mech is Sidekick 45, or 36 PP. In a PL 15 game, the pilot can be a PL 12 with some extra PP added on. Alternately, if you want to either forego Ace Pilot or grab the point from elsewhere, you can forego the Removable discount and trade a point off somewhere (maybe drop one of the Weapons Systems or some Enhanced Intimidation) to add Artificial Intelligence to the Defense Systems array. This buys off the Absent Intellect and Presence for 20 points, and exchanges the Feature from Power Dampeners to Feature 1 (Subject to technopathy effects rather than mind-affecting effects), while it is the active array slot.  
  A role playing game is three things. It is an interactive story, a game of chance, and a process in critical thinking.

  If brevity is the soul of wit, I'm witty like a vampire\!

* **Spoiler: Kill Sat (PL 15, 225 PP)**  
* Hide  
  **Abilities**

  **STR:** 0\. **STA:** \-. **AGI:** \-5. **DEX:** \-5. **FGT:** \-5. **INT:** \-. **AWE:** 0\. **PRE:** \-.

  **Stats**

  **Attack:** \+10. **Damage:** \+20. **Dodge (15):** \+10. **Parry (15):** \+10. **Toughness:** \+10. **Fortitude:** IMMUNE. **Will:** IMMUNE. **Init:** \+0.

  **Advantages**

  Accurate Attack, All Out Attack, Improved Critical (Weapons of Mass Destruction) 4, Power Attack, Precise Attack 2 (Ranged/Both).

  **Powers**

  **Armored:** Protection 10 {10}.

  **Superweapon Security:** Immunity 70 (Fortitude, Will, Technopathic Compulsion \[Limited to Non-Fort/Will Resisted; Quirk that the technopath may choose to ignore this Immunity, but if it does, must roll a DC 35/30 Will save vs. Damage Linked Impaired/Disabled/Incapacitated Affliction Linked Weaken Will for each power attempt\], Innate) {65}.

  **Gravity Wave:** Move Object 15 (Perception Range, Burst Area 4, Damaging, Selective, Feature \[Can both damage and maneuver\], Increased Mass 7, Feature 7 \[Increased Velocity\]).

  **Neutralizer:** Nullify Dreamer Powers 15 (Perception Range, Broad, Simultaneous, Concentration, Sustained, Continuous, Burst Area 3, Selective, Limited \[Effect ends for any target that leaves the area\]).

  **Diamond Shield:** Create 20 (Extended Range 15, Impervious) Linked Deflect 10 (Extended Range 16, Reflect, Burst Area 2, Selective, Accurate 8, Subtle \[Danger Sense\]).

  **Calculations**

  Abilities \-60 \+ Defenses 15 \+ Skills 8 \+ Advantages 9 \+ Powers 253 \= **225 PP**

  **Notes**

  Kill sats are the ultimate glass cannons; fragile for their PL, but with some of the most devastating weaponry on (well, above) the planet. In practice, kill sats are tricky weapons to use thanks to space fighters and defense satellites guarding, but they can wreak tremendous and tightly focused (or not) harm once moved into position. They also serve as powerful defensive weapons; a kill sat moved into position over an *invading* force can be devastating. The weakness of a kill sat is that it is, well, a satellite. It's not super-maneuverable, and while its range is tremendous, it pretty much has to move directly over its target. Highly mobile attackers will prove challenging for a kill sat. Kill sats can also provide powerful defenses to key locations, using their Neutralizers and Diamond Shields.

  Kill Sats are best known for their Ion Cannons, devastating focused beams that don't let up until the target has been reduced to ash, but they are also equipped with a formidable array of long-range attacks \- including a wide-area gravity beam that can launch targets straight into space\!

* **Spoiler: Nuke (PL 15, 225 PP)**  
* Hide  
  Equipment 225 (1125 EP).

  **Cratering Impact:** Linked Move Object 15 (Triggered \[On Detonation\], Burst Area 8, Damaging, Feature 1 \[Can both damage and maneuver simultaneously\], Limited \[Only to knock targets back or down\], Reduced Range \[Close\]) {137}.

  **Radiation Exposure:** Damage 15 (Triggered \[On Detonation\], Incurable, Secondary Effect, Alternate Resistance \[Fortitude\], Cloud Area 10, 10 ranks Cloud Area 11, 5 ranks Cloud Area 12\) Linked Weaken Stamina 15 (Fortitude; Triggered \[On Detonation\], Incurable, Progressive, Cloud Area 10, 10 ranks Cloud Area 11, 5 ranks Cloud Area 12\) {394}.

  **Fireball:** Damage 15 (Triggered \[On Detonation\], Secondary Effect, Cloud Area 12, 10 ranks Cloud Area 15, 5 ranks Cloud Area 16\) {226}.

  **Pressure Wave:** Move Object 15 (Triggered \[On Detonation\], Damaging, Feature 1 \[Can both damage and maneuver simultaneously\], Burst Area 9, 12 ranks Burst Area 11, 8 ranks Burst Area 13, 4 ranks Burst Area 14, Limited 2 \[Knockback Only\], Reduced Range \[Close\]) {181}.

  **Fallout:** Weaken Stamina 10 (Fortitude; Alternate Resistance \[Fortitude rather than Dodge to halve effect\], Triggered 22 \[Once per Time Rank that passes since detonation\], Feature 10 \[Cap Increase\], Cone Area 14, 5 ranks Cone Area 15\) {187}.

  **Notes**

  So, a nuke's a one-shot. That's why it's considered Equipment. More Equipment than pretty much any individual character can actually get (so much equipment that it counts as a character in and of itself), but whatever. It also doesn't count as making a ranged attack. The bomb/missile/whatever is *delivered* to the target site, by being dropped out of a plane or launched there on a missile or teleported there or whatever, and then someone hits a button triggering it (or it's programmed to trigger by impact or whatever) and kaboom.

  This represents about the most powerful nukes you're going to see, give or take. Lesser ones are of course possible. So, what are you looking at?

  Well, first, you get a Dodge save for half. Probably sanest to just roll one. But DCs below will be assuming full effect.

  If you are within half a mile (Distance Rank 7): Toughness DC 30 vs. \[Ballistic\] Damage, Strength or Flight DC 25 vs. knockback (or Mobility, Strength-modified if desired, DC 1d20+15 vs. Trip), Fortitude DC 30 vs. Incurable \[Radiation\] Damage (repeats next round if you remain in the area, Secondary Effect the round after) and DC 25 vs. Incurable Weaken Stamina (repeats next round if you remain in the area; no Secondary Effect, but you don't start regaining Stamina until you make a DC 25 Fortitude save, losing additional Stamina PP equal to the points failed by to max of 15 PP). Toughness DC 30 vs. \[Fire\] Damage (repeats next round if you remain in the area, Secondary Effect the round after). Toughness DC 30 vs. \[Bludgeoning\] Damage, Strength or Flight DC 25 vs. knockback.

  Within one mile (Distance Rank 8): Fortitude DC 30 vs. Incurable \[Radiation\] Damage (repeats next round if you remain in the area, Secondary Effect the round after) and DC 25 vs. Incurable Weaken Stamina (repeats next round if you remain in the area; no Secondary Effect, but you don't start regaining Stamina until you make a DC 25 Fortitude save, losing additional Stamina PP equal to the points failed by to max of 15 PP). Toughness DC 30 vs. \[Fire\] Damage (repeats next round if you remain in the area, Secondary Effect the round after). Toughness DC 30 vs. \[Bludgeoning\] Damage, Strength or Flight DC 25 vs. knockback.

  Within two miles (Distance Rank 9): Fortitude DC 25 vs. Incurable \[Radiation\] Damage (repeats next round if you remain in the area, Secondary Effect the round after) and DC 20 vs. Incurable Weaken Stamina (repeats next round if you remain in the area; no Secondary Effect, but you don't start regaining Stamina until you make a DC 20 Fortitude save, losing additional Stamina PP equal to the points failed by to max of 10 PP). Toughness DC 30 vs. \[Fire\] Damage (repeats next round if you remain in the area, Secondary Effect the round after). Toughness DC 27 vs. \[Bludgeoning\] Damage, Strength or Flight DC 22 vs. knockback.

  Within four miles (Distance Rank 10): Fortitude DC 20 vs. Incurable \[Radiation\] Damage (repeats next round if you remain in the area, Secondary Effect the round after) and DC 15 vs. Incurable Weaken Stamina (repeats next round if you remain in the area; no Secondary Effect, but you don't start regaining Stamina until you make a DC 15 Fortitude save, losing additional Stamina PP equal to the points failed by to max of 5 PP). Toughness DC 30 vs. \[Fire\] Damage (repeats next round if you remain in the area, Secondary Effect the round after). Toughness DC 27 vs. \[Bludgeoning\] Damage, Strength or Flight DC 22 vs. knockback.

  Within sixteen miles (Distance Rank 12): Toughness DC 25 vs. \[Fire\] Damage (repeats next round if you remain in the area, Secondary Effect the round after). Toughness DC 23 vs. \[Bludgeoning\] Damage, Strength or Flight DC 18 vs. knockback.

  Within thirty miles (Distance Rank 13): Toughness DC 25 vs. \[Fire\] Damage (repeats next round if you remain in the area, Secondary Effect the round after). Toughness DC 19 vs. \[Bludgeoning\] Damage, Strength or Flight DC 14 vs. knockback.

  Within sixty miles (Distance Rank 14): Toughness DC 20 vs. \[Fire\] Damage (repeats next round if you remain in the area, Secondary Effect the round after).

  Beyond sixty miles: SAFE\! Unless the wind's blowing in your direction...

  In addition, periodically from twelve seconds to eight months after the detonation, everyone within a 60 miles cone depending on which direction the wind was blowing gets a DC 20 Fortitude save vs. \[Radiation\] Weaken Stamina from fallout. Those from 60-120 miles lower the save DC to 15\. Use Fortitude rather than Dodge to halve the effect. This Weaken can reduce Stamina by a max of 20 PP (-10 Stamina), or 15 PP (-8 Stamina) in the larger spread, which is enough to Debilitate the Stamina of most Minions if they fail the save (and of low-Stamina Heroic characters if they roll really badly).

* **Spoiler: Aircraft Carrier (PL 15 Vehicle, 225 EP)**  
* Hide  
  **Basics**

  **Size:** A+. **Strength:** 24\. **Defense:** 10\. **Toughness:** \+20. **Speed:** Swimming 2\.

  **Features**

  Communications, Computer, Navigation System, Rooms.

  **Powers**

  **Tactical Computers:** Enhanced Ranged Attack 6 (Affects Others Only) {6}.

  **Heavy Armor:** Impervious Toughness 20 {20}.

  **Alt \- Ultimate Deflectors:** Immunity 20 (Uncommon Resistances \[Defense, Strength, etc\]).

  **Power Dampeners:** Feature 2 (Possesses a Will and Fortitude Defense despite Absent Abilities, starting at \-5); Enhanced Will 20 (Limited \[Non-mental Effects\]), Enhanced Fortitude 20 (Limited \[Affects Objects powers\]) {22}.

  **Computer Security:** Immunity 10 (Technopathic Control; Limited \[Half Effect\]) {5}.

  **Radar:** Senses 12 (Ranged Accurate Radius Extended 4 Rapid 3 Radio Sense); Senses 2 (Radio Sense Counters Concealment \[Cloaking\]; Limited \[Requires Perception vs. Stealth or Concealment Rank\]); Enhanced Perception 12 (Limited \[Radar\]) {16}.

  **Weapons Systems:** 108-point Array {108+6}.

  **Kinetic Cannon:** Damage 18 (Ranged, 15 ranks Burst Area 2, Extended Range 3\) Linked Affliction 18 (Dazed+Impaired/Stunned+Disabled; Fortitude; Ranged, Extra Condition, Extended Range 3, Limited Degree).

  **Plasma Cannon:** Damage 18 (Ranged, Secondary Effect) Linked Weaken Toughness 18 (Toughness; Ranged, Secondary Effect).

  **Laser Cannon:** Damage 15 (Perception Range, Alternate Resistance \[Highest Base Active Defense\], Shapeable Area 3, Subtle 2, Incurable).

  **Missile Launcher:** Damage 18 (Ranged, 15 ranks Burst Area 4, Extended Range 10, Homing 2).

  **Torpedo Barrage:** Damage 18 (Ranged, Multiattack, Extended Range 4, Homing 1, Limited \[Waterborn Targets Only\]) Linked Weaken Toughness 18 (Toughness; Ranged, Multiattack, Extended Range 4, Homing 1, Limited) Linked Nullify Swimming 18 (Multiattack, Extended Range 4, Homing 1, Limited); Improved Critical 3\.

  **Artillery Volley:** Damage 18 (Ranged, Multiattack, Targeted Burst Area 2, Indirect \[From Above\], Extended Range 11, Homing 2, Improved Critical 4).

  **Launch Jets:** Summon 12 (Fighter Jets; Active, Multiple Minions 3).

  **Calculations**

  Size 6 \+ Strength 0 \+ Defense 26 \+ Toughness 3 \+ Speed 3 \+ Features 4 \+ Powers 183 \= **225 EP**

  **Notes**

  Aircraft carriers have bigger and more advanced versions of the standard naval weapon suites, and when those don't work they can put up to eight fighter jets into the air to lay waste to their targets. Simple enough, really.

* **Spoiler: B.O.D.E.S. (Border Observation, Defense, and Ejection System) (PL 15 Installation, 30 EP)**  
* Hide  
  **Basics**

  **Size:** D.  
  **Toughness:** \+10.  
  **Features:** Communications, Computer, Concealed 3 (DC 20), Defense System 18, Intelligent (Int 0, AWE 15, PRE 0), Power System, Security System 5 (DC 40), Self-Repairing.

  **Defense Systems**

  **Detection Technology:** Senses 20 (Extended Vision 3, Analytical Vision, Rapid Vision 5, Vision Penetrates Concealment, Vision Counters All Concealment, Direction Sense, Distance Sense), Senses 10 (Acute Accurate Tracking Radius Extended 4 Awareness \[Teleportation\]) {30}.

  **Border Defense Laser:** Damage 15 (Perception Range, Selective, Reaction \[When an unauthorized subject moving at Speed 9 or higher enters the defended area from outside the country\]) Linked Affliction 15 (Dazed/Stunned/Paralyzed; Fortitude; Perception Range, Selective, Reaction) Linked Move Object 15 (Perception Range, Selective, Reaction, Limited \[Only to launch the target back the way it came\]) {300}.

  **Artillery Barrage:** Damage 16 (Ranged, Targeted Burst Area 2, Selective, Multiattack, Extended Range 9, Homing 3\) Linked Weaken Toughness 16 (Toughness; Ranged, Targeted Burst Area, Selective, Multiattack, Extended Range 9, Homing 3); Accurate 7, Improved Critical 3 {210}.

  **Calculations**

  Size \-4 \+ Toughness 3 \+ Features 31 \= **30 EP**

  **Notes**

  The BODES system is Ilessia's Border Defense Network, designed to...well, at least *reduce* the risk of foreign Dreamers, vehicles, missiles, and suchlike being able to just move right across the border. Most nations (or, in the case of the Braizen Isles and Peral, fortress-cities or city-states) have similar defenses, although Ilessia's is probably pound-for-pound the most effective.

  Each BODES tower covers a roughly 45-mile radius. They're generally situated about eighty miles apart, although along the border to Limbra it's more like forty, and positioned somewhere between fifteen and thirty miles back from the border (always at least thirty along the border to Limbra, since the no-man's-land that defines the border between the two countries is twenty-miles wide. Both networks can reach into the no-man's-land, but the terms of the treaty between the countries strictly prohibit such fixed artillery emplacements from putting the other country in their range).

  The BODES towers can be programmed to accept certain individuals, detected via facial recognition software and biometric analysis (Analytical Vision), as well as ID card auto-scanning (Penetrates Concealment so you can leave it in your pocket). Similar identification systems are in place for planes. Anything that hasn't been pre-approved which enters the protected area from outside the country will generally trigger a communication...unless it approaches at speeds in excess of 500 MPH. Past that, there isn't deemed enough time to try to figure out whether or not it's a threat, and a defense laser is automatically fired from the tower to destroy and/or repel the threat. Incoming projectiles will also trigger this response as a rank 15 Counter.

  The towers can also actively attack threats near the border with mass artillery barrages.

  BODES towers will also detect and track any teleportation into the country from outside. While they generally can't respond to such directly, unauthorized teleporters will almost certainly be greeted by a military response in short time.

  **Significant NPCs**

  **...Serving Along-SIDE:** Senses 16 (Ranged Acute Analytical Detect \[Dreamer Powers\], Ranged Acute Analytical Detect \[Technology\], Vision Counters All Concealment, Vision Counters Illusion \[Limited to Immediate Check to Disbelieve\], Danger Sense, Radius Vision, Quirk \[Individually Removable\]).

  **...Updating the Matrix with the Association of Technomancers:** Comprehend 2 (Machines), Movement 1 (Dimensional Travel \[The Matrix\]), Mental Communication 3 (Subtle, Limited \[Machines\]); Quirk (Individually Removable).

  **...Visiting the Moon with the Better World Institute:** Immunity 5 (All Environmental Effects), Leaping 1, Movement 1 (Space Travel), Flight 12 (Limited 2 \[Ascending Only\]), Feature 2 (Quick Change); Quirk (Individually Removable).

  **...Raising Beasts with the Domestic Reserve:** Strength-discounted Affliction 8 (Impaired/Compelled/Controlled; Will; Perception Area \[Hearing\], Cumulative, Secondary Effect, Alternate Resistance \[Will rather than Dodge to negate, Evasion still applies\], Quirk \[Perallan Beasts may resist with Fortitude if better\], Limited \[Animals Only\]).

  **...As Ambassador to the Tribe:** Enhanced Regeneration 10 (Limited \[Only While Outnumbered\]), Feature 10 (Can hide without cover or concealment).

  **...Training in the Champion's Guild:** Flight 8 (Quirk \[Must end movement solidly supported\]).

  **...Spying with the Secret Wardens:** Mind Reading 8 (Subtle 2, Limited \[Only While Target is Speaking\]), Senses 5 (Ranged Acute Analytical Radius Auditory Detect \[Lies\]).

  **...Swindling the Broken Ring:** Variable 3 (Technology; Continuous, Limited \[Only items that would qualify as Equipment\], Limited \[Only items that can be held in one hand\], Limited \[Change 1/scene\]).

  **Calculations**

  Abilities 64 \+ Defenses 8 \+ Skills 68 \+ Advantages 72 \+ Powers 148 \= **360 PP**
